We Found Each Other in the Dark

by mychellio

Summary

Our story begins on Halloween night where Agnes and Rio meet. Hearts are a-fluttering and feelings are a-feeling. A double murder next to Agnes's apartment leads to her being pulled into Witness Protection. Damn, and they never even got to kiss.

Ten years later, Agnes now Agatha lives in small town Westview New Jersey and as fate would have it, past meets present in the messiest of ways.

Or, Agathario Witness Protection Fic, because I want it.

Notes

Here we go again! A second Agathario Fic! Whoo!

The idea came to me and before I could stop myself I had a few chapters written down, I have zero self control...

I have to stress the fact that I am not a US citizen and English is my second language, so just live in this minimally researched world with me where places and things exist because that is what I wrote after I did 2 minutes of research on Google Maps and some university websites. I do however watch an unhealthy amount of TV and consume true crime podcasts like I do Oreos, so sometimes I think I know what I am talking about.

That being said, nobody is allowed to fact check me, because I am a sensitive lesbian with a sudden need to write fan fiction about a silly story about hot lesbian witches, and Billy.

Enjoy! Lets see where this one goes!

See the end of the work for more notes

Two Paths Cross

Rio’s POV

 

Rio Vidal loved Halloween. As a kid she had the wackiest ideas for her costumes, unfortunately for her parents, it was never just something they could get off the rack. One year she wanted to be a cheese grater, the next a pile of washing, the next a melting ice cream. Yes, she was…different, but luckily she had parents who somehow always managed to make it work, even when no one had any idea of how to make a six year old look like a plate of hors d'oeuvres. As she got older, the costumes also grew up, some were funny puns, some were political statements, and depending on the host and the potential guests, and some were down right slutty. 



She graduated from Penn State the year before, and with some dumb luck she landed her first job at Green Acres Landscape Architects as a junior architect. Fuck knows how she did that, but she was grateful, she was doing what she loved and finally making a living on her own. Plus being a woman with a decent salary did help with her personal life, she had a great apartment close to her office and all her favorite after hour hang out spots and she could impress her dates with lavish evenings around town. Rio believed her life motto to be “ Carpe Noctem”, because seizing the night was way more exciting than seizing the day.



October proved to be a difficult month at work. You wouldn't think that fall was a busy season in the landscaping business, but they had some maintenance projects and one particular big project they were preparing to start kick off as soon as spring came around. 



Even though she was up to her elbows in design proposals, Rio was still determined to enjoy her favorite day of the year, Halloween. This year she planned something more traditional for Halloween. She barely had time to think about something that would be a hit at the party, let alone get creative and make something to wear from scratch. But with a little bit of effort, she did manage to steal some time after work to put together an outfit that didn’t scream last minute costume, putting extra thought in some details of the costume to make her stand out in more ways than one. If she was going to be something more “traditional” like a witch, she was going to be the hottest witch at the party. 



This year’s invitation came from Natasha Romanoff, Rio’s one-night-stand turned best friend since college. After way too many drinks in their first year, they hooked up and when it was over, they both knew that they enjoyed the drinks and the partying together more than what followed. Plus, navigating anything relating to sex proved very difficult when both fought to top each other the whole time. What was the saying, “ Two tops does not a bottom make”... Instead they had more in common as friends. 



Just before graduation last year Natasha became infatuated with Wanda, was it the eastern European accent or their shared love for bright red hair, Rio wasn’t sure, but all Nat could talk about was her unrequited love for the girl. Rio wasn’t really interested in getting to know Nat’s latest crush, honestly the girl looked far too straight and had this Stepford Wife aura that unsettled Rio. But Rio could never resist a Halloween party. Even if the party was just a ruse for Nat to get to invite Wanda and test the waters.



“Whatever…” Rio sighed, she had a smoking hot costume planned down to the hair, makeup and character backstory, and while she finished getting dressed, securing the green hot glue gun crown on her forehead, she couldn’t help but feel a little excited about the party. She looked hot and she was ready to have a great evening. She hoped that Nat had the decency to invite someone interesting for her too, if not, their local queer bar around the corner will have to do. 



Agnes’s POV    



Agnes O’Connor hated parties. Especially themed parties with people she barely knew, and tonight was no different. She prided herself on her academic focus and that is exactly what she needed to graduate at the top of her class next year when she finished her PHD in History. She loved history, her current term paper was focused on Women's’ and Gender Studies relating to the 15th and 16th Century. She had to explain the concept to Wanda and Jen, her roommates, for probably the tenth time. 



“It's simple Wanda, the Witch Trials were some of the best recorded examples of how misogyny and sexism were used to prejudice and prosecute women. Sure we’re not flying around on brooms today, but around the world women are still being seen as second rate citizens in even the most modern countries of the world. Just because we are living in the 21st century doesn’t mean it got better for all our gals.” 



Agnes could talk about this for hours, was it a bit of a bummer in some social circles, sure, but Agnes didn’t care. Having passion for something you cared about was more important than being invited to the next major event. Unfortunately for her, she didn’t have that luxury tonight because in order to prove to Wanda and Jen that she wasn’t a bummer and a prude, she promised them that she will to go to one fucking party with them. 



It was their last year living together as roommates and they all agreed to make the most of it. Wanda was finishing her Criminal Law degree and filling Agnes’s open spot at her mother’s firm, and Jen was starting her medical internship at Northwestern soon. Agnes planned to stay on and finish her PHD despite her mother’s disappointing looks at the dinner table. 



Since Agnes changed her major from Law to History she hasn’t had the best relationship with her mother. Her mother planned on her joining the O’Connor-Calderu Criminal Law Firm once she graduated. Agnes used up every bit of courage she had and finally stood up to her mother and changed her major to something she was really passionate about. Lilia Calderu, her mother’s law firm partner and childhood friend was like Agnes’s second parent, and when Agnes decided to confront her mother, Lilia was there to soften the blow and pick up the pieces afterwards.



So there she was, standing in their shared living room dressed in her DIY costume of Anne Hathaway, Shakespeare's wife, not Princess Diaries thank you very much. Jen entered the room and stopped in her tracks as she looked Agnes up and down. 



“Ag, what the fuck? The invitation said it was a sexy Halloween party, what about this old woman drag says sexy?” Jen said, almost offended. 



“I’m Anne Hathaway, Shakespeare’s wife…” Without Agnes getting another word in, Jen ripped off part of the skirt and cut her blouse open in the front to open up her cleavage. “There, I guess you are Shakespeare's slutty wife now.”



Agnes probably looked better, but now she felt a little self conscious. She’s never been the if-you-have-it-flaunt-it type, but it has been a while since she hooked up with anyone and tonight’s party guests would probably not be the usual crowds she mingled with who would appreciate the attention to detail of her apparent  “unsexy” Anne Hathaway costume. So she accepted her fate and followed her roommates to the uber waiting outside.



When they walked into the apartment she was overwhelmed with the loud music and party guests already dancing and drinking. Taking in the costumes of the people around her, she agreed that Jen was right, her earlier costume would not have been appropriate. The host of the party approached them with a tray of shots. 



“Wanda, Jen, glad you could join,” the woman said, not really paying attention to Jen or Agnes, her eyes were fixed on Wanda and her skin tight red leotard outfit. “And who are you dressed as, gorgeous?” the woman asked Wanda, to which Wanda replied “I’m the Scarlet Witch, from the comics?” The woman’s eyes lingered on Wanda before she handed each of them a small cup of god knows what and introduced herself as Natasha. Jen took the shot and turned to Agnes to whisper “If you have any good sense, you’ll get out of her way, they’re going to eye fuck until Wanda finally gives in and no one wants to be close when that happens.” And before Agnes could reply Jen disappeared into the crowd on the dancefloor.



Next to her Natasha and Wanda were still very much in their own bubble and Agnes took that as her cue to leave. She headed towards the patio to escape the crowd and to get some fresh air, this was going to be a long night.



Rio’s POV



Being fashionably late was Rio’s forte, sure it could be seen as bad manners in some circles, but a sexy Halloween party surely lacked the decorum required to enforce any such social rules. Rio arrived just past 10pm, just in time for all of the boring people to have left and the ones who couldn’t handle their alcohol to have passed out somewhere.



She stepped into the party like she owned the place. Some girls stared in awe and some glared, she would avoid the latter she thought. Being a “Heartless Bitch” as her previous hook up screamed at her, certainly had its challenges, especially when the dating pool around the campus was drying up with women who hadn’t heard of her preceding reputation, “lick-em-and-leave-em” was Rio’s favorite accusation, she had it printed on a t-shirt and proudly wore it to campus the next week.



Rio scanned the apartment to see if she could find her friends, only to see Nat and Wanda sitting in a corner in deep conversation, Nat was clearly fighting every urge in her body to not jump Wanda’s bones. “Nope…” she mumbled to herself, looking to the other corner of the apartment, where she spotted the kitchen table lined with drinks. She’d start there. 



Rio walked over to the dining table to grab a cup of whatever Pinterest punch Nat had mixed and leaned against the table. She needed to warm up soon otherwise tonight would end up being a dud and she felt too good to have that happen. She recognized one of Wanda’s friends on the patio talking to an unfamiliar girl dressed in the most hideous slutty old lady costume Rio has ever seen. She laughed at the audacity and downed her drink and poured another before walking over to join their conversation.



“Well, well, well, if it isn’t Jane Parsley in the flesh?” Rio said as she sauntered over to the two women. 



Jen stopped talking mid sentence and rolled her eyes as she turned to Rio. “Rio, here to break another innocent heart? The night is still young.”



Rio laughed, “Oh Jane, you wound me.”



“It’s Jen Kale, you insufferable asshole. Why don’t you fuck off? Me and Agnes here are not interested in whatever drama you plan on causing tonight.”



“Right, Kale, the worst kind of vegetable” Rio said with a smirk, causing the woman with Jen to spit out her drink and laughed. 



“Sorry Jen” the woman whispered as Jen glared at her for laughing. 



“Listen Jen, I’m sorry,” Rio said, “I promise I am not here to cause trouble, you know how I get on Halloween, it’s the most wonderful time of the year!”



“Isn’t that Christmas?” Agnes asked.



“Honey no, Halloween is much better, plus everyone gets to dress up, not just your fat drunk uncle trying to score some spiked milk and cookies. This is much more fun.” Rio said, letting her eyes trace over the woman’s costume, landing on the cut open blouse. “And it is not everyday a babe like you dresses up as a sexy Anne Hathaway either, unless…”



“How did you know?” Agnes asked excitedly, as Jen rolled her eyes and left mumbling something like “ Here we fucking go again… ”



Rio smiled a crooked smile and leaned closer to Agnes “What can I say? I appreciate literature as much as the next broody lesbian… but also, you literally have it written on that sticker on your costume, so I only needed basic reading skills to figure this one out.”



Agnes glanced down at the sticker and her face turned a shade of red. “Of course. And what are you supposed to be? A slutty green demon?” she asked Rio, to which Rio replied, “No I am a green witch, specifically The Green Witch” she said, lowering her voice in a growl when she said the last part.



This seemed to spark some recognition in Agnes as her eyes lit up a bit and Rio had to steady herself as she noticed the bright blue eyes staring back at her. Whoever this Agnes was, she was beautiful. 



“You know about the Green Witch?” Agnes asked, surprised.



Agnes’s POV



Agnes stared at Rio, she was gorgeous and her costume stirred something in Agnes that she felt too unfamiliar with. Jen definitely seemed to hate this woman’s guts, but Agnes felt drawn to her for some reason. Sure she knew of her reputation, Jen complained about her enough, saying that this Rio girl kept stealing all her dates, but talking to Rio now, she didn’t see the Casanova everybody warned about. Something about Rio intrigued her, like they’ve known each other in a previous life. 



That didn’t mean that Agnes wasn’t aware that if given the chance Rio would still eat her up and spit her out, she wasn’t that delusional, but after all the drinks she’s had tonight, she felt a strange sense of confidence, and for whatever reason, Rio was interested enough to keep talking to her.



“You know about the Green Witch?” Agnes asked, surprised.



“Well yes,” Rio started to explain. “I’ve always loved Halloween, and consequently witches and Halloween go hand in hand, and I really love plants and isn’t that like her whole thing? Earth magic and all that…” Rio took a sip of her drink and Agnes swore she saw Rio’s bad girl facade slip for a split second. 



Agnes and Rio stayed on the patio talking for a while when Jen, Wanda and Nat walked over to join them. Agnes was laughing at something Rio was saying, not really paying attention to the three other women who stood staring at the two of them. 



“What’s so funny?” Jen asked. Agnes suddenly realised most of the party guests had left already leaving a small group inside and the five of them outside on the patio. Had she and Rio talked the whole night?



Rio’s face turned colder as she turned to Jen. “Wouldn’t you like to know.”



“Girls…” Nat warned. 



Agnes watched as Rio gave her a trained fake smile. She turned back to Agnes “What would you say if we ditched this joint? I know a place around the corner that stays open super late and they have the best ice cream in town. I am dying for a salted caramel cone.”



Agnes looked at Wanda, Nat and Jen who stared at the two of them like they were aliens. She looked at Rio, a genuine smile on her face, seemingly harmless and she swallowed hard before answering softly. “Okay, that actually sounds great.”



Jen and Wanda blinked at Agnes and she gave them a simple wave. “I’ll see you two tomorrow.” she said following Rio out of the apartment. She had no clue what she was doing, but there was an undeniable pull she didn’t have the strength to fight, and when was the last time she allowed herself to have salted caramel ice cream after midnight?



Rio’s POV



Rio was not going to lie, she was shocked when she realized that she and Agnes spent almost two hours just talking, as if they‘ve known each other for ages. Agnes was funny and smart, and Rio noticed small things she would do while she talked, like scrunching up her nose or when she laughed she sometimes had this cute little snort… and oh my god what the fuck was happening? Was she starting to feel something for this woman after only two hours?



Rio realized she was being too quiet when Agnes suddenly asked her where they were heading. “Oh uhm, it’s just here around the corner actually.” Rio said, pointing in the general direction of where the ice cream stand normally stood.



As they reached it, she turned to Agnes. “So what would you like?”



Agnes thought for a second and smiled, “What would you recommend?” 



“Like I said earlier, the salted caramel is my favorite.” Rio answered.



“Okay, I’ll get that then.”



Rio placed their order and waited for the man to hand her the two cones. “My lady,” Rio joked, bowing as she handed the cone to Agnes.



“Ah, a gentleman.” Agnes joked back as she took the cone from Rio. Agnes tasted the ice cream and moaned. Rio’s eyes snapped open at the sound. “This is amazing, Rio,” Agnes said as she licked the top of the ice cream. Rio swore her mouth started watering, she blamed it on the ice cream.



“It’s good isn’t it?” She said, trying to hide whatever this was she was feeling.



They sat at the fold up table and chairs in front of the ice cream stand and silently enjoyed the rest of their ice cream. Rio tried her best to not stare at Agnes, but the licking and the lingering alcohol in her veins were making it extremely hard for her not to.



“What are you doing after this?” Rio asked suddenly. She had no idea where that came from but she couldn’t stop it either.



Agnes scrunched her face as she continued to lick at her ice cream. “What do you mean, it’s past midnight?”



Rio laughed, “Yes I know, I mean like, are you going home or back to Nat’s or…”



“Or with you?” Agnes asked, lifting a brow.



Rio was sure her face was as red as the traffic light hanging over her head. “No, well. I mean you can, of course. I just meant…. Do you need a ride? We can share an uber or something?”



Agnes laughed and Rio had to fight the urge to record its sound to listen to it again later. “I’m that way,” Agnes pointed.



“I’m this way” Rio pointed in the other direction, and Rio saw Agnes’s face fall for the first time that evening, she needed to correct that immediately, “Okay, I want to make sure you get home safe, so let's take an uber to yours and then I will get one back to my place.”



“Are you… are you sure? It’s completely out of your way? And what if I want to make sure you get home safe?” Agnes asked.



Rio scoffed “Please, I am older and wiser and I know how to punch someone. I will be fine.” 



Agnes’s eyes narrowed. “Fine, but only if I can get your number.”



Rio was sure she was smiling like an idiot, but she didn’t hesitate one bit when she reached to take Agnes’s phone to insert her contact information.



They ordered the uber and headed to Agnes’s house. Rio smiled as Agnes took her hand and held it till they came to a stop.



“Mind if I text you?” Agnes asked before she climbed out of the car.



“Please do?” Rio smiled and watched as Agnes stood waving as the car pulled away. Rio’s heart pounded in her chest. This wasn’t like any other Halloween she ever had, but she felt like it was one of the best nights of her life.



Agnes’s POV



Agnes stood on the curb watching the uber disappear with Rio in it. She had the best night, and she felt giddy thinking about getting Rio’s number and couldn’t wait to send her a text. Now would be too soon, she thought. She decided that maybe tomorrow morning will be better. 



She turned to walk to the entrance of the apartment building, almost floating in a haze as she thought back to the few hours she spent with Rio, when she heard screaming coming from the alley next to the building. Normally, Agnes wouldn’t insert herself into dangerous situations, but she couldn’t stop her feet from taking her to where the screaming was coming from. 



She stood with her back against the wall and carefully turned her neck to be able to peek around the corner. What she didn’t know was that the next few minutes of her life would change everything. Agnes peeked around the corner and saw two men with their hands tied behind their backs kneeled in front of two gunmen who had their guns pointed at their heads. Another man stood next to them, clearly the leader of the pack.



“Ralph,” the one man on his knees pleaded. “I promise you man, it wasn’t us who told the cops…”



“Yeah, Mr. Bohner,” the other joined in, “We would never tell about the drugs,”



“Shut up, shut up, shut up !” the man, Ralph, screamed at them. “There is no way the cops would know about the Cargo City warehouse, and thanks to you two idiots, they raided the place and I’m out about $24 million in snow.”



“Mr. Bohner, please...” the man pleaded again.



“Jeffrey, Herb, I’m done here.” Ralph said and indicated something to the two men.



Suddenly gun shots went off and Agnes screamed running away to hide as she saw the guy, Ralph, look up towards her direction.



Agnes ran into the building and locked the door behind her, peeking through the mail hatch. She saw the two goons run around looking for her and when they ran down the street away from her she ran up the stairs and into her apartment, frantically locking the doors with shaky hands. What did she just witness? What has she gotten herself into?

Fate’s Fickle Finger

Chapter Summary

Agatha struggles to process what she witnessed and Rio, well she thinks the worst about most people, so needless to say our idiots are in a pickle. Agatha’s pickle is just way more scary.

Chapter Notes

Listen, I know I am going to get shit for timelines on this but like I said, let’s just live in this made up world with me. Our girls are losing it over ONE TEXT and here we are stressing about how long criminal trials take… bigger picture, ladies…

Agnes’s POV



Agnes barely slept, every small noise woke her up. Thoughts of the men finding her apartment and finding her kept her awake all night. When morning came she was still shaking. Jen and Wanda hadn’t come home yet, and suddenly her apartment felt too small and she had the worst feeling that she wasn’t safe with the information she had about what she had seen last night.



Deciding that she needed to leave and clear her head, she packed a small overnight bag with some essentials and sent a message on their group chat to Wanda and Jen.



“I’m going to stay at my mother’s for the rest of the weekend.” 



She called a cab and put on her best disguise, a cap, hooded sweater and sunglasses will have to do for now. She didn’t want anyone to recognize her. She walked down the stairs to the foyer of the building and hid behind the door while she waited for the cab to arrive. When it did she carefully opened the door and ran to the waiting cab, gave the man the address and shrunk into the back seat to hide herself as they drove off.



When they reached her mother’s house, she removed her disguise and walked into the house, not her favorite place to be but for now, but she figured it would be a safer place to be while she figures out what she needed to do.



She was home alone, and sat in the living room, watching some brain dead reality show, when the channel changed to the local news channel. Probably some stupid setting her mother had on the TV to alert her of possible new clients on the news. She saw the familiar building in the background of the news reporter’s frame.



“The public is urged to come forward with any information regarding last night’s double murder…” 



Fuckfuckfuckfuck, Agnes thought. She definitely had information, she saw everything happen and she still remembers all three of the men’s names. But what if they came for her, or Wanda and Jen… 



Suddenly their group chat came alive.



Wanda: “Those two men were shot next to our fucking apartment!”



Jen: “I just saw on the news, scary shit, hope you are both safe.”



Wanda: “I’m going to stay at Pietro’s for the rest of the week until this blows over. Jen, Ags, I think you shouldn’t stay at the apartment. Ag, stay with your mom okay. Jen, where will you go?”



Jen: “Uhm… I guess I could go to my parents.”  



Wanda: “Okay, I’m leaving now. Please be safe girls!”



Agnes: “I’ll stay here. Please let me know when you two are safe.”



Agnes bit at her nails. She had to do something, but knowing her mother, she couldn’t go to her, she defended guys like these, she probably even knew them. She had to figure something out, she couldn’t live with this secret eating at her.



Rio’s POV



Rio watched the news on the gym’s TV in front of her, not really concentrating while she ran on the treadmill. She saw the news of the double murder, not recognizing anything particular about it and jumped off the treadmill wiping away the sweat off her forehead. She checked her phone again. Rio really hoped to have gotten a text from Agnes, but nothing yet. She could have kicked herself that she didn’t also get her number but she thought she would give the girl time. It was still early and she didn’t want to push too hard. If need be, she could just ask Jen or she could ask Natasha to ask Wanda… fuck, this was high school all over.



She hoped to hear from Agnes soon, in the meantime she would distract herself at the gym.



Agnes’s POV



Dinner with her mother was always an event she dreaded, but given the circumstances she bit her tongue at every snide remark as they discussed her term paper and final year ahead at Penn State.



“I know it doesn’t sound as glamorous as criminal law, mother, but I love it. And I am doing very well. Dean Smith says that there might be a staff position available for me next year if I keep my grades up, and that actually sounds perfect. I can build my own curriculum and teach, what more would I want?”



“I don’t know Agnes, it seems like a waste. You are too smart to be… staff.” Evanora said snidely.



Agnes took the hidden compliment as a small win and finished the rest of her dinner in silence.



Lying in her childhood bed didn’t bring the safety she wished it had, she woke up from nightmares every few minutes. This continued into the next night. She had to go to the police, she couldn’t do this anymore. 



The day before, she watched the news again in hopes that there may have been another lead or something, but the police had nothing and were still in the dark. Has no one else come forward yet? Agnes wrote down the anonymous tip line number and sat with the number dialed in her hands. She just had to press the call button…



Without thinking too long about it she pressed the call button and heard the phone ring.



“PPD tip line, how may I help?”



Agnes hesitated…



“Hello?” the voice answered.



“H-hi I have some information…” she finally spoke. Her hands were shaking and her heart was pounding.



“Ma’am, are you in a safe space to talk?” the woman asked.



“Y-yeah, I… it's about the shooting. The one near campus.”



“Please hold…”



Agnes thought about dropping the call, when another voice sounded over the phone. “Hi ma’am, this is Detective Jones, I understand you have some information about the campus shooting?”



Agnes answered “Yes” and proceeded to give the Detective every bit of information she had. Even the names of the men she overheard at the scene, the name she heard about the warehouse, everything she knew. 



In an hour the detective and some other police officers were at her mother’s home. Thank fuck her mother was out for the day.



“Ma’am for your protection I will need to move you to a safe house. If they saw you, they will be out looking for you. You will not be safe at your apartment.”



“Can’t I just stay here?” she asked.



“If you are willing to testify at the trial, we can't risk them knowing about you. We will keep you safe until the trial is over, it will be for your own safety and that of your friends and family.” 



Rio’s POV



A week passed since Halloween night, and Agnes still hasn’t sent Rio a text and she started feeling like she had been played. “ Fuck that chick, there are more where she came from” she thought as she sat in Nat’s apartment nursing beer when Nat plopped down on the couch next to her. 



“So? What are we getting up to tonight?” Nat asked.  



”I need to get drunk, so whatever you want to do, I’m doing that.” Rio said, taking a long sip of her beer. 




*****



Rio sat across from Nat at their regular bar, staring at the drink in front of her. She couldn’t shake the gnawing feeling of irritation or disappointment that Agnes never texted her. They didn’t even hook up and now she was hung up on her. She wasn’t even her type, she was beautiful yes, funny for sure, a bookworm, a mouthy feminist and not all as outgoing as the girls she usually sought out. Why did she have such a fucking hold on her?



“Rioooo?” Nat yelled, knocking her out of her inner thoughts. “Am I talking to myself tonight?”



“Sorry Nat, I’m just in my head tonight….” Rio shook her head and downed the last of her beer. “Another round?” She asked as she stood up.



“Yeah, sure, you’re buying…” Nat replied.



Rio ordered them another round at the bar and walked back to their table. She had to talk to Nat, if only to get Agnes off her mind. “So,” she tried “How are things with Miss Wanda?”



Nat sighed, “Honestly, it’s very frustrating, I keep getting mixed signals. One day we’re flirting like crazy and I think yeah this is happening and then then next day it’s like we’re both in a knitting circle struggling with small talk, like, how’s your grandson doing, Mary?” 



Rio laughed at Nat’s old lady voice “Yeah, that’ll confuse me too. Have you tried telling her you like her?”



“I mean, am I not obvious enough? I only spoke to her at the party last week and we text and call each other the whole time. Apart from yelling Wanda I fucking like you, I think I’m pretty obvious.”



“Maybe she doesn’t know, maybe she thinks since you flirt with almost everyone, including the furniture, that this is just what you do, you know. Maybe you need to be more forward, like actually ask her on a fucking date.” Rio suggested.



“You might be right, Rio…” Nat considered Rio for a few seconds, “But what’s been up with you the last week, I mean here we are, alpha predators at our watering hole, and you haven’t even attempted to hit on someone, and let me tell you, blondie over there has been eyeing you since we sat down.”



Rio turned to look in the direction Nat was pointing at and saw a very attractive blond girl staring at her. She waved and turned back. “I don’t know Nat, I’m… tired I guess.” Rio didn’t want to bring up Agnes, tonight was about getting her out of her head, and she hasn’t succeeded for even one minute.



“Something is up, you’re quiet, and almost… timid. It’s starting to freak me out actually. You’re not… dying are you?” Nat asked, feigning concern.



Rio blew out some air and laughed, “No… it’s just…” Rio rolled her eyes, maybe it would help to ask, Nat knew Wanda and Wanda knew Agnes, maybe they talked… “So you remember Wanda’s friend Agnes?”



“Don’t tell me you hooked up with slutty grandma?” Nat asked curiously.



“No we didn’t, and she wasn’t slutty grandma. She was slutty Anne Hathaway.”



“Like the actress? I don’t see it…” Nat looked confused.



“No, Shakespeare’s wife, Anne Hathaway…”



“Who?”



“Never mind… anyway. So the night of the party we talked, a lot actually, and then we went for ice cream afterwards, you remember. Then I went home with her and gave her my number and its been like almost eight days and nothing, not even a hey thanks for the salted caramel, please leave me alone forever. Like nothing.”



“So you’re butt hurt over a librarian girl you didn’t even kiss?” Nat asked .



“I know, what the fuck is wrong with me.” Rio asked, slapping her forehead lightly. “For some weird reason, I can’t shake her.”



“It sounds like you can’t stand the fact that you met the only other woman, apart from me of course, who is immune to your wiles.” Nat teased.



“As I remember correctly, you were not so immune when my fingers were all up in your…”



“Yeah okay, okay!” Nat interrupted. “So what? You want me to ask Wanda to ask her if she likes you back, like junior high shit?”



“No, I guess, I just want to know why she… disappeared on me. Like we had a good time, we were having fun and she did say she’ll text me. What if I left her in a ditch when I left in the uber? I don’t know, I have a weird feeling about her.”



“Well actually, Wanda and Jen had to leave their apartment after the double murder last week. You know it happened right in the alley next to their apartment building.”



“You’re kidding, I thought the building looked a bit familiar on the news.” Rio leaned forward.



“Yeah, it’s crazy, so they are staying away for now, it's only temporary, but I assume Agnes probably did the same. Wanda said it’s only till the coast is clear and the trial starts.” Nat paused for a bit. “I saw on the news, they caught the guys, some anonymous tipper gave the police exactly what they needed to catch them. Wanda said the trial was starting next week, pretty fucking fast, so you know thise guys are bad news.”



“Yeah it sounds like it.” Rio couldn’t help but think of Agnes. Was she so affected by this that she had to get away? 



“But I will ask Wanda if she knows, maybe she’ll even give Agnes’s number to me?”



“Would you mind? I just want to check in. If she tells me to fuck off I’ll do it.” Rio said. 



Agnes’s POV



The safe house was… fine. It was more like a dormitory, but Agnes felt safe enough. She told her mom she was staying with friends and she told her friends she was staying with her mom. Classic high school shit. 



The prosecuting attorney came over to discuss her testimony in preparation for the trial. When this is finally over she could get back to normal. The trial would start in a week, record timing apparently, but she was told that they had been building the case against Mr. Bohner for years and her final testimony was exactly what they needed to put him away for life. 



In the meantime Agnes caught up with some of her assignments. She thought back to that night. It started out so perfect and she actually liked spending time with Rio and then her fucking curiosity went and messed everything up. Why did she have to go to the alley? Why didn’t she just go into her apartment and just text Rio?



Now, ten days later, a text out of the blue will make her look like a pathetic asshole, plus she wasn’t technically allowed to contact anyone outside of the prosecution team. So she was in a bind. She wishes she could have had the chance to explain to Rio why she had gone silent. Now nobody knew she was here and she couldn’t tell anyone anything. 



Rio probably forgot about her anyway, sure they had fun, but nothing really happened and why would Rio be interested in her anyway. She had a reputation as being a big flirt and Agnes thought of herself as being… plain in comparison to the girls she thought Rio usually liked. She didn’t want to flatter herself by thinking that Rio was somewhere out there pining by her phone for a text from Agnes. That wasn’t happening.



Over the next few days the prosecution team rehearsed her testimony and went over the last details before the trial. 



“Will they know it was me?” Agnes asked nervously.



“Agnes, you will be in court in front of the defendants. Your testimony will most likely result in a guilty verdict, and we can’t assure you that they will not be able to retaliate, but we will certainly do our best, whatever the outcome. You will be safe.”



“What if I am not? They’ll know who I am, what my name is, it’s not that difficult to track someone these days if you have basic information about them.” Agnes felt sick.



“Let’s just focus on the trial and your statement next week, okay? We need to be sure that whatever you say in court will put them away otherwise all of this would have been for nothing.”



Agnes didn’t feel any less stressed about the trial. If anything she wishes the last two weeks never happened, and she felt completely alone. She wished she could call Wanda or Jen, fuck even her mother or Lillia. She just had to make it through the trial and one more week. That’s what the prosecutor said, one more week.

Gone with the Wind

Chapter Summary

We're heading for a collision, past, say hello to present!

Chapter Notes

See the end of the chapter for notes

Agnes’s POV

 

One more week. That turned into two. Fuck that felt like a lifetime was passing before her eyes. The trial was a complete mess, but her testimony had the necessary evidence for the jury to decide that Ralph Bohner and his two goons were found guilty of murder. After her testimony the man jumped up and tried to get closer, only to be dragged away in handcuffs yelling over his shoulder “You’re a dead bitch Agnes O’Connor!”



Agnes remembers the cold shiver running down her spine when she heard her name being shouted as he was being dragged away. And to make things even worse, the defense lawyer was no one other than her own mother dearest, Evanora O’Connor. 



A conflict of interest that should have prevented her mother from representing them, that was expertly explained away with only the years of experience gained from defending the absolute worst of society. She expected nothing less from her mother. The fear and absolute betrayal she felt at the time sitting in court facing her mother, as the co-council cross examined her would haunt her forever. 



After the trial Agnes was taken to a quiet room in the courthouse. She was reeling from what just happened. Her mother defending the murderers, her mother using everything she knew about her to get her to crack, and then the death threat after the verdict. 



Surprisingly, Lillia managed to sneak in to talk to Agnes before the police and prosecution team came in to debrief her after the trail.



“Agnes, if I had known…” Lillia said, concerned. “Your mother never said you’re the witness. She should have never allowed this to happen, to cross examine you like that. It is unheard of, I am surprised she got away with it.”



“How could she defend him? He’s a monster Lillia! He’s literally threatening to kill me and she just stood there. She was more concerned about losing the case than she was about her own daughter’s life.” Agnes burst out crying. “What’s going to happen to me now? I can’t go out there, he’s still got people on the outside, he knows where I live, he knows my name…I can’t even trust my own mother anymore.”



“There are protections available for you Agnes, and I’ll make sure of it. I promise.” Lillia tried to console her but nothing she could say was going to change the fact that her life was in actual danger and she felt completely isolated and alone. 



Lillia kissed her on her forehead, promising to make sure she was okay and snuck out of the room just before the detective and prosecutor entered the small room she was waiting in.



“Agnes, we need to talk about what happened here today.” The prosecutor said, “Obviously we aren’t taking it lightly that your life may now be in danger. Ralph Bohner is a powerful man and we can’t be certain that he won’t have contact with his gang members outside of prison.”



“Wha-what does that mean, exactly?” Agnes asked.



“We’re getting you into the witness protection program. You’ll be moved to a safe place, under the supervision of one of our agents, and when enough time has passed you will be able to come back.”



“I’m sorry, I don’t understand. How long will I be away? And what about my family, my friends and my degree. I have a life here!” Agnes felt like her world was collapsing around her. 



“We don’t know how long Miss O’Connor, but we’ll be able to set everything up from here. Your background story, your home, new identity. We have counselors who help with the transition. They will also assist with the story you tell the people you are leaving behind.”



“Leaving behind? Do you mean, I am breaking contact with… with everyone and everything I have ever known? Is this a joke?”



“No Agnes, this is life or death. You can refuse but we can't guarantee your or your loved one’s safety otherwise.”



Agnes was sobbing, what was fucking happening? This couldn’t be real! One moment she was on cloud nine after having one fucking ice cream with Rio, and weeks later she was being shipped off to god knows where with a new identity and a new life.



“This isn’t fair! He’s the fucking murderer and I am the one paying for it!?” She screamed in frustration.



“The program is there to protect you Agnes. It’s been done more times than you will ever know. And most people get to return to their old lives after a while.”



“Can I at least call someone? Do I have any say in how and when this happens?” Agnes was pleading now.



“It’s protocol to remove you from any and all danger as soon as possible, unfortunately that time seems to be… now. While we can still move you without Ralph’s people knowing. They’re probably scrambling after the verdict, so we should strike now.”



Agnes was at a loss for words. Unfortunately that time seems to be now. The words spinned in her head over and over again eventually nothing made sense anymore, and somewhere in between the blurry words in her vision, a smirk and two dark brown eyes were staring back at her. Rio.



Rio’s POV



“What do you mean she’s gone ?” Rio asked Jen confused.



“I thought she was still staying with her mother, but no. When we got back to the apartment after the trial, all her things were just gone, three month’s rent was in an envelope on the coffee table with a note saying that she got a job offer she couldn’t refuse and that she had to leave immediately. Believe me I am pissed. She just fucking left, no goodbye nothing.” Jen said angrily. 



Wanda was crying, “I can’t believe she just left like that, I mean I thought we were close. We lived together for three years! Not even Lilia can tell us what happened.”



Rio was dumbstruck. “I barely knew her, but I guess I was blindsided. Bullet successfully dodged.” 



Nat clinked her bottle with Rio’s. “Looks like it babe, if she could pick up and fuck off that easily, she was definitely not going to waste her time with you.”



The table was silent for a while. “It’s just strange,” Rio said contemplating something, “When we spoke, she had plans, you know. There was the staff opening in the history department at the university, her PHD, I mean I guess you could do that anywhere, but the way she spoke about her friends and her life here… she didn’t seem like the type to pack up and disappear in the middle of the night. Did you go to the police? Maybe she was kidnapped by those gang guys?”



Wanda nodded, “We did, actually. They said they were able to reach her and confirm that she was alive and didn’t want….” Wanda started crying again.



“Didn’t want contact…” Jen finished for her.



“Well fuck,” Nat said exhaling, “I guess you never really know a person.” 



******Ten years later******



Agatha’s POV



Agatha Harkness hated Halloween. In a previous life she had one memorable Halloween night and after that her life wasn’t her own anymore. She stood in the small costume rental shop in Westview, New fucking Jersey, where her seven year old son was trying on a costume of a hot dog od all things. This kid had a sense of humor like no other. She pulled her driver’s license out of her wallet and stared at it while she waited, she almost recognized the younger face staring back at her. She barely remembered her old life. Now Agnes O’Connor was more like an old school friend who she lost touch with over the years. 



“Mom, do I look like a real hot dog in this?” Nicky asked. The foam costume looked ridiculous but Nicky insisted. 



Agatha laughed, “You sure do! Is that the one you want?” 



“Yup,” he said laughing at himself in the mirror.



“Okay, we’ll take the… hot dog suit.” Agatha said to the lady behind the counter. 



“Excellent choice.” She winked at Nicky. 



Agatha squeezed the suit into the trunk of her car and climbed into the driver seat. “Ready to go to your mother’s?”



“Yeah, she and Melinda are taking me trick or treating tonight. It’s going to be so much fun! I wish you could come with us, though.” Nicky said.



Agatha loved her son, but spending the evening with her ex and her new girlfriend wasn’t exactly what she thought would be a good time. “You mother loves Halloween way more than I do, kid. Just go and enjoy yourself this week, okay, I’ll pick you again up next Sunday afternoon.”



“Okay, mom.” Nicky said.



When she moved to Westview she became Agatha Harkness. High school history teacher, relocating from the big city to small town New Jersey for a simpler life. Somewhat believable. People downscaled constantly.



Her Witness Protection agent, Alice, was the only person she knew, but they soon developed a friendship and Agatha started feeling less alone. Her new job as a history teacher at Westview high wasn’t as exciting but she learned to love the kids in her classes. She also helped out with the after school programs assisting the drama teacher, Mrs. Davis, who insisted that she join the teachers for drinks after the first school play she helped with. That night she met Maria Hill, the science teacher.



They went on a few dates and before she knew it, they were engaged and eventually married. Alice was the only person Agatha invited to their wedding. Two years later, Agatha gave birth to their son Nicky. Five years later, after many fights and tears, mostly Maria‘s, they decided to get a divorce. They had a much better relationship as exes actually, it turned out and Agatha also  liked Maria’s new girlfriend Melinda May. True to lesbian fashion, her circle of friends now consisted of Alice, her ex wife and her girlfriend. What a fucking joke.



After Agatha dropped Nicky off at Maria’s she decided to go to the bar down the road from her house, she had the whole weekend and week to herself and she didn’t feel like spending it in front of her television tonight. 



Agatha sat at a small table hidden away in the bar, reading a book and nursing a big glass of red wine while she waited for Alice to arrive. She probably looked fucking ridiculous reading at a bar at 4pm on a Friday afternoon, but the bar was quiet and the wine was good enough. 



“What the fuck are you doing here?” She heard a familiar voice suddenly. When she lifted her eyes up from her book she saw no one other than Jennifer Kale.



“Jen?” She said, taking off her glasses. Just then Alice walked up to Agatha and she saw the two women staring at each other. “W-what are you doing here , Jen?”



“I think I asked you first, Agnes.” Jen scolded.



“Don’t… don’t call me that here please.” Agatha whispered in a hurried tone. 



“Oh fuck,” Alice said, sitting down quickly and grabbing at Jen’s hand to pull her down into the seat next to her. “Agatha, do you know Jen?”



“Yes,” both Agatha and Jen answered at the same time.



“Fuck okay, uhm before anyone says anything else. Let me just make a call. Jen baby, could you please get us some drinks?” She asked. Jen baby? Agatha thought hearing the term of endearment for the woman. “And Agatha, stay here and don’t talk to anyone until I tell you to.”



Agatha was so confused and the way Jen was staring at her from the bar, she knew she wasn’t the only one trying to make sense of it all.



Alice and Jen came back to the table at the same time and took their seats again.



“Before we start, Jen, I need you to stay calm as I explain this okay?” Alice said cautiously.



Agatha was still staring at Jen, her friend from ten years ago, now sitting in front of her, holding her Witness Protection agent’s hand while she was explaining the current twilight zone they were sitting in now.



“…so after the trial, they had to evacuate the witness, Agnes, and relocate her to a safe place, here, where they gave her a new name, Agatha, and I was assigned to be her WPA, easy as that.”



Agatha simply blinked and sipped her wine as she listened unphased as Alice explained the events leading up to the end of her life as she knew it in less than five minutes. As if she was listening to a gardening podcast, she numbly took another sip of her wine. “There you have it, the story of how Agnes became Agatha.” She said plainly.



Jen stared at her, silently studying her. She narrowed her eyes, “We fucking hated you, we burned your pictures after a night of drinking too much, hell I think we even cursed you the next Halloween.” Jen laughed nervously.



Agatha smiled a sad smile, “Well I think it worked, I am fucking cursed. I’m a divorced lesbian history teacher, living in the middle of nowhere with exactly five friends which sadly includes my WPA, my seven year old son, his mother and her girlfriend and a sixty year old drama teacher who’s name I keep getting wrong. Really living the life here.”



“Ha!” Alice laughed awkwardly.



“I can’t believe you were here all this time? Do you know I work at Mount Sinai Hospital now, it’s less than an hour from here, and in ten years, I never run into you, until I agree on coming to my girlfriend’s local bar for Halloween, to meet her old friend, which turned out to be… you.” 



“Small fucking world.” Agatha mumbled into her wine.

Chapter End Notes

I hope we all get used to the Agnes/Agatha name change. I had to edit this three times to make sure I got them all. Also, take a shot every time you read Ten Years.

Safe as Houses

Chapter Summary

Jen lets Rio know about her encounter with Agn-atha…

Chapter Notes

And here all those with knowledge of US maps can kindly forget what you know. My fic, my map.

See the end of the chapter for more notes

Rio’s POV



Rio woke up with a throbbing headache. The late afternoon sun pierced through the small opening in the black out curtains she haphazardly pulled closed after stumbling into her room at 2am this morning. Another fucking Halloween party. Why was she still going to these parties? She couldn’t answer that. Maybe it was hope, maybe she was just pathetic. 



It has been ten years. Ten Halloween parties. Three failed relationships. One big wedding, not hers. Four promotions to partner at the firm and absolutely zero fucking texts from Agnes. It was sad actually, no it was fucking pathetic, Rio should donate her brain to science because never in the earth’s existence has any being been this fucking pathetic. There are worms without brains or eyes that are less pathetic than Rio, who after meeting a woman once ten years ago, still couldn’t get her out of her head.



Pah-the-tic!



And has she tried? Yes, the list of blocked numbers on her phone would be enough proof on its own. Her last relationship ended just weeks ago, what could she say? The woman wasn’t Agnes and she was extremely boring. Nat and Wanda’s wedding had a few attractive distractions, which was fun for a while, but as hot as the sex was, the woman had the sense of humor of a potato. Rio was doomed. Doomed to compare every woman she ever met with the one that seemingly got away, the one she never even had more than a few hours with.



Rio rolled out of her bed, feeling like death warmed up and hung onto the fridge door as she willed the contents in her fridge to magically turn into breakfast other than just ingredients. She grabbed the jar of peanut butter and bread and proceeded to make some toast. She needed to get groceries. Absentmindedly she scrolled through her phone, when suddenly it started ringing.



“You will never believe where I am right now!” Jen whispered from the other end of the line.



“Good afternoon Rio, how are you Rio? That is how you start a call or did you lose your fucking manners when you moved to New York?” Rio said, taking a bite of her toast.



“It’s almost 5pm Rio, and are you already drunk? Isn’t it Nat’s party tonight?” Jen said bluntly.



“No, that was last night, they have theatre tickets or something gay like that, so Halloween had to move, oh and if you called just to shit on me and tell me the time, I’m hanging up.” 



“Rio, I found her!” Jen whispered louder this time.



“Who? Your other personality?” Rio joked.



“No you asshole, Agnes!”



Rio dropped her phone on the counter, no on her peanut butter toast, screen side down of course, but she could still hear Jen’s muffled voice through the peanut butter. 



“Hold on Jen, I… I’m putting you on speaker.” Rio picked up her phone and froze for a second, she quickly licked enough peanut butter off the screen to put the call on loudspeaker. “What do you mean you found her?”



“You’ll have to come here. I swore to Alice I wouldn’t tell you anything over the phone.” 



“Jen, I am so fucking confused.” Rio hung her head and scrunched her face. “Come where?” 



“I’ll send you the details. But Rio, tell no one. Not even Nat and Wanda. Just, get here as soon as you can, okay?”



“Jen, what the fuck? Do you expect me to come to wherever you are, based on absolutely no other information other than a get here now and a lovation pin?”



“Yes,” she answered bluntly.



“And who the fuck is Alice?” Rio asked, frustrated.



“That's…. not important now. Look Rio, just get here, okay. For ten years we had to sit and listen to your one-that-got-away monologues and now that you might finally get answers or closure you are being fucking difficult.”



Rio considered everything Jen just told her for a moment. “Fine. Send me the location.” 



Rio watched as a pin and an address appeared in her inbox. She clicked on the pin. Fuck it was three and a half hours away. She’ll be there in less if she pushes it.



Agatha’s POV



The bar was starting to fill up more, some patrons were dressed in their Halloween costumes and others were simply here because what else was there to do on a Friday night in this small town? Alice came back from the bar and slid another glass of wine in front of Agatha. Jen was still in the ladies room and Agatha wondered what was taking her so long.



“So what now Alice?” Agatha asked. “Now that my cover is probably blown…”



“Agatha, an old friend running into you is not a blown cover, we just have to try and keep the lid on it, you know, if one person knows, depending on the relationship with that person, nothing needs to change. But that means we have to try to keep it to only one person.” Alice explained.



“Okay, well we’ll have to tell Jen that, she’s always been a gossip.” Agatha smiled, remembering her old friends and how they would sit around and chat and gossip in their shared living room.



Just then, as if summoned, Jen emerged from the ladies room and sat back down at the table.



“Are you okay?” Alice asked, “You were gone for a while.”



“Yeah, I just took a minute, you know, to… process. It’s not normal to find your ex-best friend again after she disappeared ten years ago.” Jen said. Something in her voice was off, Agatha couldn’t place it, but she hasn’t been around her for so long, so maybe this is Jen now. 



Agatha remained quiet. Like Jen, she was processing. But unlike Jen she lost a lot more than just a friend back then. Without so much as a decent goodbye she packed up and left her whole life and future career behind. After ten years, it felt like she was still processing that .



“So, Agatha, what is your life like here, now?” Jen looked genuinely interested, like she really was trying to get to know her again.



“Oh uhm… I teach history at Westview High, I help with the drama club after school, I got married then divorced and have a seven year old son and a rabbit. Nothing exciting. Just the regular hiding from drug gangs and murderers in small town New Jersey kinda stuff, you know.” Agatha said dryly. “But tell me about everyone else?”



Jen blinked, “Okay… well Nat and Wanda finally got together, they married like three years after you left. I ended up in New York for my internship and now I’m in the oncology department… oh and your mother, she and Lillia had a very public separation of their firm, after the trial your mother got dropped from the bar, something about ethical violations, Wanda would be able to explain this better, but your mother sort of disappeared after that and now Lillia and Wanda have their own firm.”



“Wow, I… fuck I missed out on so much.” Agatha felt the tears welling up in her eyes. “Wanda got married? And my mother, she disappeared? Do you even know if she is okay?” 



“Wanda says Lillia has people who know things, who keep track of people. I wouldn’t be surprised if she knew where you were.” Jen said, taking a sip of her drink again. 



“Doubt it…” said Alice flippantly.



Agatha actually missed her mother even though she could never forgive her for defending Ralph Bohner and his goons. And Lillia, the woman who provided a safe place when her own home felt like a war zone, she really missed her too. And Wanda’s wedding, she always said that she was going to be a bridesmaid, but she never got to share this with her friend. Hell, she couldn’t even share her own wedding with them, even though it didn’t work out. But really, she was trying to fight what she actually wanted to ask Jen about. Rio. 



“But in all honesty, Agn… Ag, Wanda would probably never bring it up anyway, you know, I mean we missed you and talked about you a lot but it… hurt, we thought you left and didn’t want to know us anymore. And Rio…” Jen stopped talking suddenly, Agatha wanted her to continue, she wanted to know what was going on in her life too. “Well now that I know where you are, we could maybe catch up? Is that allowed, or something you would even want?”



“You kind of have a big mouth Jen, I might have to kill you to keep you quiet. I don't need you blabbing to the world where I have been hiding out.” Agatha joked trying to break the tension. “But if it is allowed, I would actually love that. I really don’t have a lot of people here that I can stand for long enough to have an actual friendship with, except Alice, but she gets it.“ Agatha smiled at Alice, “But technically she is being paid to be my friend, so who really knows if this friendship is real?” 



Alice bumped Agatha’s shoulder “You know I love you, Ag, but I must admit, the check in the mail does make it a bit more bearable.” she joked. 



The three women laughed and ordered another few rounds, the bar got fuller and by 9pm they were more than enjoying themselves. Many things may have changed in the last ten years, but Agatha’s love for karaoke never did, and she could put up quite the performance. She was on stage drunkenly singing Crazy on You by Heart and just as she was in the middle of her air guitar solo she looked up from the stage and then she saw her. Rio.



Rio’s POV



As soon as Rio received the address of the bar in Westview she grabbed what she needed and jumped into her car. Her GPS said the drive to “Tony’s Liquor and Diner” was 3:27 hours exactly, but Rio’s Range Rover would be driving faster than the speed limit today, she’ll worry about the speeding tickets later. All she could think about was how she needed to actually see Agnes, to know that she was okay, and then she could throw one of Tony’s fine beers straight in her face and drive back home. Dramatic, yes, but she couldn’t explain the pull ten years ago and that same pull was in charge now.



The road was long. Rio left just after 5:15pm and would probably be there by 8pm at least. She turned up the radio and took another drag of her cigarette, she was nervous. Where has she been all this time? What has she done? Was she happy? Did she regret leaving the way she did? Did she even think about her?



These questions mulled over and over in her head, no matter how many songs she sang at the top of her lungs, every thought started with one of those questions. Rio sighed in relief as the sign on the side of the road finally read “ Welcome to Westview: Home is where you make it ” The irony didn’t escape her. 



A few miles past the sign she saw the flashing signage of Tony’s. She pulled her car into one of the few open parking spaces, the place looked very busy. Well it was Friday night in the middle of nowhere and it was Halloween, so it made sense for people to be enjoying themselves tonight.



Stepping out of the car she started to hear the sounds of an obviously drunk person butchering one of her favorite Heart songs. Karaoke was both a blessing and a curse sometimes , she thought. She entered the bar and looked for Jen, then her eyes were drawn to the person responsible for the loud cheers, and there she was, Agnes, obviously drunk but obviously enjoying herself with her air guitar solo. Without thinking about it, she slowly walked to the front of the stage and stared up into the same bright blue eyes she remembered from exactly ten years ago. Agnes.



Rio watched as Agnes dropped the microphone and froze, the karaoke backtrack of the song was still playing but Agnes stood still and stared at Rio like she was a ghost. Finally the song stopped playing and that seemed to break her out of her stupor. She watched as she walked to the stage stairs, picked up a drink from a small table, downed the contents of the glass and walked towards Rio. No, she walked past her and pulled Rio’s arm for her to follow.



She was being pulled outside and followed almost in a trancelike state herself. Her body moved by without her telling it to. Outside she stopped and watched Agnes as she stepped ahead a little further away and stopped with her back still turned to her. The woman standing in front of her seemed so different yet so familiar. Rio didn’t move, she simply stared and waited. 



As if a switch had flipped, Agnes turned around and walked to Rio with purpose. Before she had time to respond, to look, to move away, soft hands grabbed at her face and soft lips met hers instantly. When her brain finally caught up with her body, she threw her arms around Agnes and pulled her closer, returning the kiss that she had been wanting for for the last ten years.



Agatha’s POV



Agatha kissed Rio, her body wasn’t hers. She felt like she was watching it all happen from far away, but she felt it, god did she feel it, Rio’s soft full lips dragging over hers, Rio’s hands and arms pulling her closer, Rio’s warm breath blowing through her nose tickling her skin. 



Suddenly everything felt too much. She broke away from the kiss and stepped away, putting a few feet of distance between herself and Rio.



“Fuck sorry, I shouldn’t have, I didn’t mean to…” she started apologizing.



Rio didn’t move, she stood in front of Agatha, looking at her like she was staring at nothing and everything at the same time, her mouth slightly open. 



“Agn…” she heard Rio start but she was interrupted when Alice and Jen suddenly came out of the bar. 



Agatha looked at Jen. “ You called her?” She asked almost angrily.



Jen looked like she was caught breaking into a bank. 



“Fuck, who else knows, Jen? This was a mistake, I… I need to leave.” Agatha said. She was fighting not to cry but the fear and her tears were starting to build up. She turned around and started stumbling forward on the way to her car.



“Agatha, wait,” Alice yelled. “You can’t drive, you’re drunk.” 



Agatha stopped in her tracks and pressed her hands to her eyes. “Then I’ll fucking walk.” 



Before she could turn to walk into the direction of where she thought her house would be she heard Rio say, “I’ll drive you.”



The four women stood still, Agatha felt their eyes burning holes through her body. “Fine, whatever.”



After another few silent seconds Agatha asked, “Well? Am I walking or what?” 



Rio fiddled with her keys and shared a quick look with Jen which Agatha wished she could interpret, her brain was too foggy to comprehend anything at the moment. Agatha followed Rio to a big black Range Rover. “Wow, this is your car? Are you like rich rich now?”



Rio laughed as she helped Agatha into the passenger seat. “I mean I do okay,” 



“Pfft, if this is doing okay, my life is even more pathetic than I thought.” Agatha mumbled.



“Come on, let’s get you out of here.” Rio said before closing the door.



Agatha sat in the car, it was fancy, way better than her little sedan she was driving. She watched Rio walk to the driver’s side and get in. “So where am I driving to?” Rio asked her.



“Just go straight and turn left at the first street.” Agatha was pointing in the general direction of her house and felt the car come alive and pull away.



“Turn here,” she said, feeling the car turn into the street. “And then right here.”



“Wow,” Rio said as they stopped, “You really could have walked. The bar is like less than a mile from here…I think I can still hear the music actually.”



“I know, but you were insistent and I am in no condition to fight you.” Agatha said, pulling up her fists as if she was going to fight. 



For a moment they sat in the car and Agatha sighed and suddenly felt her stomach turn. “I think I am going to be sick,” she opened the door and stumbled out, almost immediately feeling her hair being pulled back and being guided to the garden.



When she was done, Rio gave her a tissue to wipe her face. This was fucking humiliating, she thought. 



“Where are your keys?” Rio asked helping Agatha up.



Agatha pulled the keys out from her pocket to gave it to Rio. “You have to wiggle it a bit.” Agatha said shaking them in front of Rio’s face.



Agatha followed Rio to the front door, watching her wiggle the keys in the lock and opening the door for her. She walked to the sofa and plopped down into the cushions. When she opened her eyes after a brief second, she saw Rio standing frozen in the doorway. 



“There are some drinks in the fridge, help yourself.” She gestured to the kitchen.



Rio walked to the kitchen and when she came back she held two beers and a bottle of water. “I don’t know if you should still be drinking, but you make your own rules.” She put the beer bottle and water bottle on the table in front of Agatha and sat down in the high back chair opposite her.



Agatha looked at the two bottles on the table, she considered drinking the beer but the water would help sober her up a bit and she felt like she already fucked up enough tonight. So she grabbed the water and drank half of it before putting it back onto the table. 



Rio looked at Agatha with concern, or was it confusion or worse was it indignation? “Don’t look at me like that, Rio.”



Rio leaned forward and placed her beer onto the table. “You have a son?”



Agatha smiled, “Yeah, Nicky. He is seven.”



“Okay, and you have a rabbit?”



“Yup, Señor Scratchy, his more Nicky’s than mine.”



“And you are Agatha now.” The way Rio’s mouth shaped the name felt weird.



“That’s what my papers say.” Agatha raised an eyebrow. The name wasn’t that bad. “I went from one old lady's name to another. Seems like Witness Protection ran out of cool names like Kathryn or whatever.”



“It still suits you.” Rio said quietly. “Witness Protection… is that what this is… why you left?”



Agatha considered Rio for a moment. This was already crossing so many lines. In one night she blew her cover to not one, but two people. But this was Rio , and whatever force drew them together that night was still here, alive and well.



“That night we met, you left with the uber and I heard yelling and for some fucking reason I went towards it and saw the two men get shot and killed. I heard everything and they saw me, I had to testify in the trial and when they were convicted they threatened my life and before I had any chance to process what happened I was already placed in witness protection. So now I am here, Agatha Harkness, high school history teacher who needed a break from the big bad city and chose the butthole of New Jersey as my soft landing place to start a new life.” Agatha couldn’t help the bitterness in her voice.



“It wasn’t all bad, in the beginning I cried a lot, I mean I lost everything I worked for, everyone I loved, and I was so alone.” Agatha drank the last of the water in the bottle. “Alice was my appointed agent and we soon became friends, I met and married Maria, we were happy for a while and then came Nicky, and then we divorced… and now I am sitting here in front of the one person I never thought I’d ever see again.”



Rio laughed, Agatha stared at her. “I’m sorry, is my fucking life a joke to you?”



“No, no, I think I just… do you know how much this has fucked me up? And here you are, a three hour drive from me, completely the same but completely different.” Rio stopped laughing and her face turned serious. “I thought I imagined you, you disappeared like you were never even real, but I never stopped thinking about you, about your fucking words that have haunted my thoughts every day for ten years “ Mind if I text you…” . I have waited for that text since that night.” Rio’s head fell into her hands. 



Agatha opened the beer bottle in front of her, she didn’t drink from it, she simply held it in her hands. “I begged them to let me call someone, to let me call you.” Agatha wasn’t looking at Rio. “You never deserved feeling like I ghosted you or whatever.” 



“And you never deserved…this.” Rio finished.



“Yeah, well, it’s not all bad. I had Nicky and that made up for most of it. I think without him I would have jumped off the water reservoir halfway through my time here…”



The two sat quietly for a while, taking in everything that just happened. “Do you need a place to stay?” Agatha asked. “There is a spare bedroom with its own bathroom through the door there.”



“I think that will be okay, if you don’t mind. I didn’t really think this through when I drove here.” Rio admitted.



“You’re more than welcome,” Agatha stood up and headed for the stairs. “Use what you need, I will see you in the morning.” Agatha walked to her bedroom and heard the guest bedroom door open and shut. She fell onto her bed and softly cried herself to sleep for the first time in years.

Chapter End Notes

Anyone still with me, there are still a lot of "Ten Years" in this one… hope we’re all still standing by the end.

Time Waits for Nobody

Chapter Summary

Rio starts snooping for some ideas and who else knows all the town gossip other than our Teen?

Chapter Notes

Thank you for the nice comments so far, it warms my damned heart....

Rio’s POV

 

Waking up in Agatha’s home felt surreal. In total, the amount of actual hours she has spent with Agnes/Agatha since they met, was only about fifteen hours if you include the hours of sleep she just woke up from. That number is insignificant if you calculate the percentage over the timeline of ten years. A drop in a very big bucket of time, but Rio has never felt a connection this intense with anyone before. 



And the kiss, however unexpected, felt ten years overdue. It wasn’t perfect at all, it wasn’t even that long. It was hurried, and sloppy and drunk, but it was needed. Rio didn’t realize how much she wanted that kiss to happen until it finally did. And now she needed more, under better circumstances of course, but now that she finally knew what Agatha felt like pressed up against her, cupping her face and the feel of her lips on hers she needed that again, she needed more .



Rio had to remind herself that Agatha had been drinking the night before and if there was anyone on earth who knows how fast things can happen after a few drinks it was Rio. Maybe it was just that, a drunken kiss, an impulsive decision based on the sudden reappearance of an old flame, if that was even what she was. Something impulsive that she will most likely regret when she realizes what she has done. Also, not one word was said about it after it happened. Did it even happen? It had to have, her lips still felt the ghosts of Agatha’s.



She rolled over in the bed and stared at the painting on the wall. It was one of those generic paint blob paintings you would buy to fill up an empty wall. No meaning or thought was put into the design and it was mass produced to hang in every other home across the country. Somehow the painting felt out of place in the room she was lying in. Everything else looked deliberate. Some pieces of furniture looked more used than the rest but they were probably carefully selected and purchased from some second hand store in town. Unlike the painting the room was warm and felt like Agatha. She had made a home for herself in this house, Rio realized. Another life here in Westview. Even after the disruption of being forced to relocate and start over, she found a way to still have something warm.



Rio wondered what Agatha’s bedroom would look like. She wondered if it also felt personal and warm, like she remembered her to be that first night. Rio shook her head and got up to walk to the bathroom. She needed to take a shower to help clear her thoughts.



Agatha’s POV



Agatha heard the shower in the guest bathroom turn on. Something about knowing who was behind the closed doors of the room stirred something in her. Her head was killing her and the sound of the effervescent tablet dissolving in the glass in front of her was almost too loud.



She thought back to the events and the conversations of the night before. And the kiss, she acted completely on impulse and pure need . Her stomach turned, but not from her hangover but rather because of her past and her present colliding all at once. She buried Agnes O’Connor the day she set foot in this house. She mourned the death of her and her life and her friends and family she had to leave behind. Now, seemingly resurrected, they were no longer just ghosts or suppressed memories, they were all too real again. 



It was a complete coincidence that Jen showed up with Alice yesterday, and then Rio who came after Jen called her. But coincidences don't just happen like this, and that was what was eating her up. If she was this easy to run into accidentally, how easy will it be for Ralph’s gang to find her, to find Nicky? She picked up her phone and sent a text to Alice.



“ We need to talk. About RB.”



When she heard the shower turn off she decided to get some breakfast ready for her and Rio, if she was staying that is. Maybe she should just start with coffee. Agatha turned to the coffee machine and started a brew. If Rio wanted to stay for breakfast she'd make something quick and easy, and if she wanted to leave, Agatha would be fine to pour out the extra coffee and move on with her day.



As if on cue, the guest room door creaked open and Rio, dressed in only the t-shirt from the night before and her underwear, peeked out of the room.



“Uhm, I forgot my bag in the car last night.” She said softly.



Agatha couldn’t help but stare at the pair of toned legs sticking out from under the shirt. “I can get it.” she offered. 



“Thanks,” 



Agatha smiled shyly as she walked, almost stumbling past her to the front door. She took the car key and went outside. The crisp November air hit her squarely in the chest and she took in a deep breath to steady herself. She opened the car and found the small bag of clothes haphazardly thrown in the back of the Range Rover.



When she walked back into the house Rio was sitting on the sofa, scrolling through her phone. She gently put the bag down next to the guest room door. “I made coffee, if you’d like some.” 



“Thank you, that will actually be great. Let me just get dressed.”



Rio hopped up from the sofa and disappeared back into the guest room. Agatha let out a breath. Her hangover combined with the storm in her mind was making her feel sick all over again. 



Her phone buzzed on the counter. She expected a text from Alice, but instead it was from Maria.



“ Check out our Hot Dog” 



Two pictures of Nicky dressed like a hot dog were sent after the text, one with him smiling wide next to Maria and another of just Nicky pulling a funny face. She laughed at the picture and saved the second one to her camera roll.



“The coffee smells great.” Rio said as she walked over to the kitchen. Agatha poured her a cup and slid it over to her on the counter. Rio was wearing fitted sweatpants and a loose t-shirt, she looked effortlessly casual and attractive at the same time. 



Agatha poured herself a cup to distract herself from staring too long. “Are you hungry? I don't have many options but I can make toast and eggs or if you need a sugar rush, Nicky’s cereal will definitely do the trick.”



“Hmmm. What cereal?” Rio smirked, looking interested in the second option.



Agatha huffed out an amused breath and opened the pantry pulling out a box of cereal, which could only be described as sugar coated sugar balls. “He loves this and I know it’s bad for him, but he was such a fussy eater when he was smaller that I tend to give in to him when he finally decides to actually eat something. Don’t tell his other mother that.” 



Not surprisingly, Rio chose the cereal and Agatha made herself some toast with jam. She watched Rio pour the milk over the sugary cereal and like a giddy kid she took a big spoon full. Agatha smirked while she took a bite of her toast. “Do you always eat like this?”



“Hey, sugar is an important part of the food pyramid. Your kid has good taste, this is quality cereal.” Rio said with a mouth full. Agatha snickered at that. Who was this woman she barely knew but felt so familiar with?



Agatha’s smile lingered on Rio for a moment, “You are like a child.” 



Rio grinned, “You have no idea, Agatha.”



Agatha shook her head and put the dirty dishes in the sink to deal with later when she felt less like an alcohol soaked rag. 



“So what does the lovely town of Westview have to offer for entertainment to the odd tourist passing through?” Rio asked, propping up her chin on the palm of her hand.



“Well there is Tony’s, a fine establishment of course,” Agatha mocked, “Then there’s a pretty decent coffee shop and bookstore, there’s a small roller rink that doubles as the rec centre for bingo nights on Wednesdays… oh and the drive in on Saturdays. They mostly show older movies, but it’s not bad and Nicky loves it.”



Rio tapped her chin with her pointer finger. “Okay, and if said tourist wanted to take someone out, something special?”



Agatha narrowed her eyes, silently analyzing the line of questions coming from Rio, “The Italian restaurant on the town square seems popular for dates. It’s not a five star restaurant but it’s really nice authentic Italian food. The miniature golf course is quite popular for the kids at school… But honestly, I don’t really go out much so I wouldn‘t be of much help.”



“Do you mean to say that you, Westview’s own karaoke queen, don’t go on dates? Are the women here blind, straight or both?”



Agatha felt her cheeks turning pink, she hadn’t been on a date since before Nicky was born. “Please, this town’s queer population is almost non-existent. With you and Jen in town we might be able to finally start a soccer team, but we'll probably still be short one player.”
