It’s Almost Over

Chapter Summary

The chapter's title sums it up.... We're almost home my babies.

Rio’s POV



After getting the “all good” and a thumbs up from the EMT’s and finishing both their statements with the police for the fender bender, Alice and a fleet of officers and FBI agents arrived at the gas station. When they pulled up, tires screeching and guns pointed at nothing and no one, Rio simply rolled her eyes and muttered below her breath to Agatha, “Right on time to get the undeserved credit…”. Another line of police vehicles flew past the station in the direction Agatha came from, most certainly on their way to the house where Evanora and Ralph definitely wouldn’t be at anymore unless they weren’t as clever as they thought.



“Morons,” Rio snarled at the police vehicles flying by the gas station.



Alice stormed over to them, obviously furious, but a visible relief washed over her the minute she pulled Agatha into a hug in the back of the ambulance. Agatha groaned and brushed off her injuries as she explained what happened, but the worry and the fear of “What now?” still sat deep in her eyes, deeper than the small cut above her brow from the accident. 



Alice held onto her as she walked them over to the car with Rio following behind them, too angry and emotional herself to really engage with Alice. As Alice held the back door of the SUV open for Agatha to get in, Alice turned to Rio. Both their eyes communicated in silence to the other, one saying “Don’t you ever try that shit again” and one saying “I told you I would find her by myself”.



It seemed like the second Agatha’s head touched Rio’s shoulder in the back of Alice’s car she was out. Rio could feel Agatha’s body finally relax against her as she drifted off to sleep. Rio held onto her hand, loose enough to not cause any discomfort, but tight enough to remind her that she was safe, that Rio was here and that she wouldn’t ever let her go. Rio made that promise to herself and decided she would make that same promise to Agatha, as soon as they were home and safe again. For now Agatha was sound asleep, tucked under Alice’s coat to keep her warm against Rio’s side.



The car was silent except for the soft music playing over the car’s speakers. Rio recognized the song and silently mouthed along to the lyrics. Lucy Dacus singing about making up for lost time felt fitting. Rio would make up for their lost time, for the last 10 years since they met on that Halloween night and also for the awful few days they had spent apart now. “But I will, I would, I did, I do. For the thrill, for my health, for myself, for you.”



Along with the silence between Alice and Rio, a thick atmosphere hung like a dense cloud over them in the car as they drove back to Lilia’s from the gas station. Every now and then Alice would steal glances in the rearview mirror, sometimes checking on Agatha still slumped against Rio’s side and other times meeting Rio’s eyes only to dart away awkwardly, back to the road in front of her. Rio felt it, there was a big ass white elephant in the car with them, but honestly, Rio wasn’t really angry, but she couldn’t help the tiny bit of resentment she felt towards Alice. 



Obviously it was unfair to have those feelings of resentment towards Alice, she was really just doing her job and following protocol, but in Rio’s mind and heart, there wasn’t any protocol on earth that would have kept her in that house, especially not after they found Agatha’s location. Knowing where Agatha was and not knowing what Evanora would let them do to her if she were their hostage any longer would have driven Rio fucking insane. 



“It’s okay if you need to hate me, you know.” Alice said quietly, meeting Rio’s eyes again in the rearview mirror. Rio barely caught the words over the low drum of the music still playing in the car.



Rio sighed as she shifted awkwardly and felt Agatha move against her side. To be honest, Rio didn’t really know what she felt other than just the relief of finding Agatha and having her safe by her side again. “I don't hate you Alice.” Rio said with a sigh, “I mean, you found her, I could never thank you enough for that, but you have to know, I couldn’t sit around and wait for you to go and get her.”



“You know the minute I got the location we had a team ready to go, but we needed to do things right..” Alice said, turning her head slightly towards the back. “If we had made just one mistake…”



“I know, you had your protocols.” Rio rolled her eyes and stared back out of the car’s window as they passed the “Welcome to Westview” sign. “You have to understand Alice. I’ve lost her once already. She vanished without a trace. I wasn’t going to let that happen again.” Rio wiped a tear from the corner of her eye and cleared her throat.



Alice’s eyes met Rio’s once more in the mirror. “You know, if we had to wait for the warrant much longer, I would have done the same.” Alice smiled. “Fuck protocol.”



Rio smiled back at her and nodded. “Yeah?”



“Oh definitely. But I probably wouldn’t have literally run into her like you did. You two could have killed each other.” she laughed. Also, my tank is always full.” Alice smirked as she continued.



“Fuck, I couldn’t believe it when I saw I was running out of gas. I mean, who keeps an empty car in a fucking safe house?” Rio laughed as she shook her head in disbelief.



Alice huffed out a silent laugh, “That place was too flashy for a safe house anyway. Who needs a fucking stable and a lawn the size of a small polo field when you are hiding out.” 



“I guess when you are one of Lilia’s rich white collar criminals, a dingy apartment in an unknown town just won’t do.” Rio chuckled.



Their laughter died down. “Will we be safe there now?” Rio asked wide eyed. “I mean they breached your security once…”



“We’ve amped up the security and have more bodies on site. Also, we have eyes on Evanora and Ralph now. It’s just a matter of time before we have them both in custody.” Alice was using her agent voice again.



“Keep me away from your laptop, unless you want me to find her myself.” Rio joked.



“You know you won’t leave.” Alice smiled, hinting at Agatha.



“No, not this time.” Rio said, gently squeezing Agatha’s hand.



The bit of banter and laughter they shared the rest of the way to Lilia’s helped to further ease the tension between them and by the time they pulled into the courtyard of the safe house Rio’s demeanor towards Alice relaxed. In the end both of them cared for Agatha and both of them only wanted her to be happy and safe. 



Alice got out of the car and met some officers guarding the front door while Rio stayed behind in the car to wake Agatha to take her inside. Rio moved gently below Agatha’s head and lightly brushed her fingers over her cheek to wake her up. “Agatha baby, we’re here.” Rio whispered against her forehead as she placed a soft kiss above her brows where the small cut was bandaged up.



Agatha blinked to wake slowly and scrunched her face as her hand reached up to her head. The pain medicine the EMT gave her was probably wearing off already.



“Let’s get you inside, yeah?” Rio said, unbuckling them and opening the door. She ran over to the other side to open Agatha’s door and help her up and out of the car.



“Nicky?” Agatha muttered.



“It’s past 2am, baby, he’s asleep already, but Maria is here with him, he’s okay.” Rio said, holding onto her side.



Agatha nodded sleepily and allowed Rio to lead her inside. Rio helped her up the stairs and to the bedroom they shared before the incident and sat her down on the bed.



“What do you need, my love?” Rio asked, gently cupping her face.



“Can I please get out of this filthy pajamas?” Agatha huffed, “And a shower. Fuck, I need a fucking warm shower.” 



Rio laughed and bent down to kiss her. “Okay, why don’t you get in the shower and I’ll get you new pajamas and something to drink and snack on before bed?”



Rio kissed her quickly and turned around to go to the kitchen. 



“No! Don’t!” Agatha said, almost too loud and too quick. 



Rio froze mid step and her head snapped back to Agatha.



“Don’t leave.” Agatha pleaded with her hand stretched towards Rio. Her voice broke quietly and Rio’s heart broke along with it as she watched Agatha’s eyes start to fill up with tears. “Don’t leave me please. I can’t… I don’t want to be alone again.”



Rio felt a tear run down her face and hunched down to fold her arms around Agatha who cried silently into her shoulder. “Okay, baby, I’m here. I won’t leave you alone again, I promise.”



Rio held Agatha like that until her frantic breathing and heart rate slowed down to a normal speed. “Let me just grab something clean for you to sleep in, okay?” 



Rio walked over to the closet and took out her favorite sweater and joggers and helped Agatha to change out of the grimy pajamas she had worn for the last three days. She threw them straight into the bin, they’ll get her new ones. Agatha’s shoulders relaxed instantly and she climbed under the covers of the bed she probably missed a lot more than Rio could imagine. 



When she was settled Rio cleaned the old glass she had on her night stand to fill it with water for Agatha, but before she could return with the glass of water Agatha was back to sleep already. Rio quietly placed the glass on the night stand next to her and walked around the bed to her side before getting in behind her. She turned off the bedlamp and folded her arm around Agatha’s waist, curling into her back. Agatha shifted under her hold and pressed herself tighter into Rio’s front.



Rio kissed Agatha’s cheek and closed her eyes for the first time in what felt like forever since Agatha was taken. Finally, Agatha was safely back in her arms where she belonged.



“Thank you Rio...” Rio heard Agatha mutter in her sleep. “...for finding me.”



“I’ll always find you my love.” Rio whispered, pulling her in tighter. “Always.”

Agatha’s POV

 

Agatha’s head was throbbing when her eyes opened. For a split second she thought she was back in the dusty basement but the room was lighter and warmer and she smelled coffee and something that made her stomach grumble. She was starving, she realized. 



Agatha felt a warm body behind her back, a steady rhythm of warm air blowing against her neck, tickling her every now and then. A lazy arm draped over her waist and held her tight in comfortable closeness. She slowly turned under the arm and carefully moved to sit up in the bed. Rio moved in her sleep, not lifting her arm off of Agatha’s middle. Agatha felt her hand twitch against her stomach as she rustled under the covers next to her. 



Agatha stared at the sleepy body beside her. Rio’s face was scrunched up against the comfy pillow and even in her sleep she had a small frown between her brows, as if she was even scrutinizing her own dreams. Agatha stretched her arms up and looked down at the sweater she was wearing. It was one of Rio’s. A worn sweater printed with “Salem Witch Trials 1692. You missed one.”



Agatha grinned and smiled. Only Rio would wear this with absolutely no shame. On second thought, she would probably have bought the exact sweater for herself. But Rio’s was warm and comfortable, and more importantly, it smelled like Rio. She’ll just have to keep it, she smirked to herself.



Agatha chuckled a bit too loud at herself and suddenly Rio’s eyes flew open. Agatha saw her panic as her eyes opened wider than necessary and she sat up quickly. “You okay?” she muttered concerned, still sleepy.



Agatha laughed and brushed her hand to Rio’s cheek. “Morning, yes I’m okay. I promise.” Agatha smiled lovingly at Rio who instantly relaxed and settled back down onto the pillow she was sleeping on. “My head is killing me though, and I will eat my pillow if I am not fed something decent within the next fifteen minutes.”



Rio laughed and rolled over closer to Agatha. “Let me just hold you a bit.” 



“Rio. I love you sweetheart, but I will eat you too.” Agatha said, not really joking.



“Promise?” Rio smiled and bobbed her brows up and down.



Agatha swatted her away and stood up from the bed, almost losing her balance. Her head was killing her and she felt dizzy. “Shit…” 



Rio was by her side in a second. “Easy, your head. The EMT said there might be some dizziness. You okay?” Rio asked Agatha as she steadied herself against Rio.



“Yeah, I’m… okay.” Agatha said, blinking up at Rio. Rio gave her a soft kiss and lingered against her lips. Agatha had to pull herself away from Rio, they’d catch up with that later. “I missed you.” Agatha whispered. She hummed and kissed Rio again, “I want to see Nicky and can I please eat something.”



“Yes, my love.” Rio laughed, “Let’s get you fed.”



Agatha and Rio walked hand in hand down the corridor and down the stairs, more careful than Agatha would normally allow, and when they walked past the living room towards the kitchen, Agatha heard Nicky call as he ran up to her. “Mom!”



Agatha fell to her knees instantly and her tears spilled from her eyes as she caught Nicky. “Nicky, my love!” Agatha said between kissing every part of his face. “Nicky… god I am so happy you are okay.”



Maria and Lilia stood in the doorway and watched the reunion with teary smiles. Rio’s hand was anchored to Agatha’s shoulder and Agatha held Nicky as tight as he allowed her. “Mom, I missed you!” he said. “Mom said that you didn’t want to leave me and you were going to be okay, but I was still scared.” Agatha was fully crying now, tucking a small curl away from his face. 



“I would have never left you my love. Never.” Agatha hugged him tight and felt Rio’s hand squeeze her shoulder. She was so thankful to be safe and back with her family.



“Let’s have some breakfast.” Lilia broke the silence. “Nicholas, they made pancakes.” 



“No way!” Nicky gasped excitedly. He freed himself from Agatha’s arms and ran to the breakfast table.



“Well, I guess pancakes trumps returning mother.” Agatha joked.



“It’s always been his kryptonite.” Maria laughed. “Glad you are safe, Ags.” Maria said with a heaviness in her voice. The sadness and guilt was all over her face.



“I’ll meet you at the table.” Rio said, kissing her cheek.



Agatha turned back to Maria and reached out to hold her hands. “Are you okay?”



“Ha,” Maria laughed tearily, “I’m not the one that was abducted.”



“You are allowed to feel sad Maria,” Agatha said quietly. “I know Mel…”



“I’m sorry, I should have trusted you, listened to you.” Maria admitted as she interrupted Agatha.



“Maria, you couldn’t have known.” Agatha comforted her. “This is not your fault, okay.”



Agatha sat down between Nicky and Rio at the breakfast table and when a fresh mug of coffee was placed in front of her she almost cried again. “Fuck me, I love coffee…” Agatha said, instantly bringing the mug to her lips. 



“Language mom!” Nicky yelled.



The table erupted in laughter and what followed was the best breakfast Agatha has eaten in ages. Not because of the food, but because of the family around her. Being back safe next to her son and Rio. Her friends, Maria and Alice and her aunt, Lilia. Agatha almost lost this, but she didn’t. Now she was going to make sure she never will again.



In the Aftermath

Chapter Summary

Agatha settles into being back after everything

Chapter Notes

Guys listen, I know, it's been a whole ass month.

Apologies to those hanging on for an update!

But here you go, I added some spice in the end... hopefully it will be enough to hold you over until the next chapter drops.

Agatha’s POV



Agatha hoped the nightmare was over after returning to the safe house. The morning after she spent with her loved ones around the breakfast table and it felt amazing. She thanked all the stars above her to be able to have that again after what her mother almost got away with, but an undeniable feeling of dread was still hanging over her. Sure she got away, she escaped, but that didn’t mean she was safe. Not until Ralph and Evanora were finally behind bars.



For the rest of the day after her return, Agatha spent almost every minute of the day in some form of interview with the FBI and local police repeating statement after statement. It reminded her so much of the first time she had to go through this, but fortunately this time she had Lilia by her side acting as her council. 



“This time will be different dear, you have me and I am an incredible lawyer.” Lilia assured her with a wink. “Only answer what is necessary, let them fill out the blanks and I’ll do the rest.”



Agatha answered each question quickly and carefully and when she rambled too much, Lilia stepped in, nudging her with her knee if she maybe gave too much. Just like she was promised, Lilia would handle the rest. Nothing was said about dead bodies. Nothing was mentioned about any vehicular theft. Lilia made sure of it. When it seemed like the questions were leading one way, Lilia steered them back on track. In the end, they got what they came for and finally left Agatha to rest.



That night she felt completely drained after having to relive everything that happened over and over again with each interview and eventually she passed out on the sofa next to Rio, who held her as they watched some mindless television after dinner. Agatha only woke up the next morning in bed next to Rio who probably carried her to bed the night before. She couldn't even remember that happening, but she was thankful for her, for having her here.



After breakfast the next morning, the house quieted down as everyone kept busy for what would hopefully be the last day of staying in the safehouse. Rio took some quiet time to work on her new business plan and Lilia offered her the office for the day. Agatha wandered in and out of the office, stealing kisses every now and then. She couldn’t stay away long, not while Rio was typing away with adorable concentration and her tongue poking the side of her cheek, deep in thought.

 

The last time Agatha came in, she couldn’t stand it anymore and closed the office doors behind her and quickly walked up to Rio, straddling her lap in the office chair only to kiss her deep and languidly, a promise of what to come once they’re finally alone again. 



She let out a low frustrated moan when Lilia walked in on them, only clearing her throat and pretending to not see them. Agatha felt the tips of her ears burn in embarrassment and reluctantly climbed off as if nothing happened and walked out, leaving Rio smiling awkwardly at Lilia. Agatha left Rio to work after that. 



Maria and Nicky were sitting in the lounge, reading under a fluffy blanket while the fireplace crackled quietly across the room. “We fucking got them Ags.” Alice smiled proudly.

“Funny story actually.” Alice said with a soft chuckle. Alice continued explaining, “Looks like someone called the tip line a few hours after that video of you went live on the news, saying that they saw suspicious and violent activity around that area. Coincidentally, the address they gave matched a property we had on file. A direct  link to your dear mother Evanora the terrible. Cops arrived on the scene the next day, finding Ralph and Evanora scrambling into the van matching the description Rio gave the detectives.”

“It was anonymous, but I have my suspicions.” Alice smirked. “I asked around to find out where the call came from but they wouldn’t tell me. But the caller did ask for only one thing in return…which in my opinion says enough…”

“No, they actually declined the reward. They only had one request. Well, one message to give to you.”



“And?” Agatha said skeptically.



“To tell you that they were sorry for betraying you for all these years.” Alice let her sit with that for a while.

She heard Maria correct him as he struggled with another difficult word and heard Nicky give a frustrated sigh only to restart the sentence again.  



Realization hit her just then and she turned back to face Alice again. “It was Melinda, wasn’t it?” 



Alice smiled, quietly confirming to Agatha.



“She turned on them?” Agatha asked.



“Like I said, the caller wanted to stay anonymous.” Alice shrugged, feigning nonchalance. “I’m not really supposed to tell you, but you’ll find out soon anyway. The news channels will be all over this anyway. You’ll have reporters all over you soon enough…”

“The police arrived as Ralph was carrying a body into the black van, obviously trying to get rid of the bodies and other evidence around the property.”

They found the one guy in the house, his head was smashed in against the kitchen counter, and the other guy was stabbed in the neck with a small sharp object.”

So thanks to your mother…”

“Thanks to her witness statement, and Ralph obviously trying to hide evidence and move the bodies, it was apparently clear as day. Cops almost closed the case on the spot and charged Ralph for the two murders. But Ol’ Mother And Evanora’s not getting away scot-free either.”

“Nope,” Alice said, popping the p. “They’re both in holding now, probably being booked and prepped for trial, which I don’t think will be too long from now either.”

Alice hesitated for a minute, unsure of what else she could share, but continued anyway. “Actually, Melinda helped a lot with that. She shared a lot of evidence. Years of payment history, incriminating message threads… Evanora might be innocent of actual murder, but the FBI’s case against her is strong. They’ve got her Ags. It's…”
